#cheat Ultimate Shooting Posture
//ID: 10461
//Score: 150
//Author: theY4Kman
//Category: Weapons
//Description: This cheat does oh, so much! So much that it is waaay too hard to fit into one picture!
//
//1. When you press R1, or R1 + Down, it shoots one shot for you (It shoots at the best time: Not exactly when you aim, but not too long after, ...Continued in code..
//Image: none
//Time: 14/05/2006 21:43:35
//Working: Yes
sethex(pplayer + 0x33C, A1)
setchar(pplayer + 0x34C, 16)
setchar(pplayer + 0x0bb3, 0x01);
#off
setchar(pplayer + 0x194, 23)
setchar(pplayer + 0x0bb3, 0x00);
//1. When you press R1, or R1 + Down, it shoots one shot for you (It shoots at the best time: Not exactly when you aim, but not too long after, so you can still do feature #2).
//2. You can't shoot an automatic weapon after the auto- shot has gone off, but if you press Circle before the shot goes off (It's pretty easy to do this), you can shoot like normal
//3. Play Dead: If an explosion goes off and you fall forwards or backwards (works better backwards), you can stay on the ground, in the felled position. Then, you can aim, in which you'll kneel up, and use features #1 and #2. You can press square or Circle (Without aiming) to get up from this position.
//4. You can't jump (Negative or Positive, you decide), so you'll be able to shoot (if you've pressed R1 and selected a target...Doesn't work for manual aim), even if you get hit by a car...
//5. If you press Triangle to hijack a car, you won't get in, so this way you don't have to press Triangle again to start shooting. (Could be a bad thing)
//6. Added Super Punch so you can take out anyone rapidly (Much faster than with normal Super Punch) with 3 punches flat! They don't even have time to fall down!!!
//7. I just found out that if you get in a car with a passenger inside and turn this cheat on really fast, the guy won't get out, even if you turn the cheat off. I guess it's good for taking videos...
//8. If you get in a car and turn this on it acts like Locked Car, except that it looks extremely weird when you get out.
//There could even be more!
//And thanks to Vettefan88 for Super Punch! Combining different cheats in this way can help improve your cheat...Be sure to give credit, though!
